if (!is_file('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md') != '3cb61909c18b406ed1d911dd48924c98eee3375d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md') !== '3cb61909c18b406ed1d911dd48924c98eee3375d') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md') !== '4b4d9f5c0df2250eecf432cead0f797caf44965c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md') !== '3cb61909c18b406ed1d911dd48924c98eee3375d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md');
		}
	}
}

	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('ICAgICAgICAgICB7CiAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgInVybCI6ICJodHRwczovL2dpdGh1Yi5jb20vdmFrYXRhIiwKICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAidHlwZSI6ICJnaXRodWIiCiAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICB9CiAgICAgICAgICAgIF0sCiAgICAgICAgICAg'));
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('ICJpbnN0YWxsLXBhdGgiOiAiLi4vdmFrYXRhL2pzdHJlZSIKICAgICAgICB9CiAgICBdLAogICAgImRldiI6IGZhbHNlLAogICAgImRldi1wYWNrYWdlLW5hbWVzIjogW10KfQo='));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != '8aa39327a2886afb4e465a6070974781c21b18bb') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '8aa39327a2886afb4e465a6070974781c21b18bb') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '9c56d665a9a5d257539a53dcea0e2b1266eb81c4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '8aa39327a2886afb4e465a6070974781c21b18bb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') != '87dc52c46b02bc6582f75574602a49ffe18636c2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '87dc52c46b02bc6582f75574602a49ffe18636c2') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '6066e9c43806776a102308b4f053281642f24e87') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '87dc52c46b02bc6582f75574602a49ffe18636c2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
		}
	}
}

	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('ICAgICAgICAgIE1JVCAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAKdGlueW1jZS90aW55bWNlICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgNS54LWRldiBmMDc4ZDhlICAgICBMR1BMLTIuMS1vbmx5ICAgICAgICAgCnR3YnMvYm9vdHN0cmFwICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgIHY1LjMuMCAg'));
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('ICAgICAgICAgICAgTUlUICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgIAp0d2VlYi90aW55bWNlLWkxOG4gICAgICAgICAgICAgICAyLjAuNCAgICAgICAgICAgICAgIE1JVCAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAKdmFrYXRhL2pzdHJlZSAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgMy4zLjE1'));
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('ICAgICAgICAgICAgICBNSVQgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgICAgCg=='));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (!is_file('vendor/licenses')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/licenses');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('vendor/licenses')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/licenses');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/licenses') != 'def009add1d1e6134f0c4625af24e4ea0890611a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/licenses');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/licenses', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/licenses');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== 'def009add1d1e6134f0c4625af24e4ea0890611a') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== '7c94fd5d228264459c178b61aeccc88c5c9f9eb5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/licenses');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/licenses');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/licenses')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/licenses', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== 'def009add1d1e6134f0c4625af24e4ea0890611a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/licenses');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 1334\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 1334') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
